1️⃣ Multi-Deck Offsets
Rule: Each deck is treated as a volume module that contributes to hull protrusions and silhouette. Decks can be:

Vertical stacks: Classic top-down multi-deck

Side expansions: Lateral wings for additional bays or fab spaces

Rear offsets: Stern modules for ramps, elevators, or cargo bays

Exterior Mapping:

Deck Type        | Exterior Cue
-----------------|-----------------------------
Vertical Stack   | Main hull mass, clean vertical poly layers
Side Wing        | Angular protrusions, struts for support
Rear Offset      | Ramp bay doors, hull overhangs
Multi-offset     | Readable modular silhouette, varied panel angles
Procedural Rule: Each deck offset creates a convex hull extension, then snaps to parent deck grid. Child modules (bay, fab, drone bay) inherit the deck’s position.

2️⃣ Ramp / Elevator Placement
Rule: All ramps or elevators are functional interior modules that produce readable hull cues:

Ramp Modules: Generate sloped polygons on exterior, door outlines

Elevators: Generate vertical airlock panels, reinforced sections, mag-lock or hatch details

Procedural Mapping Table:

Interior Module   | Exterior Cue
-----------------|-----------------------------
Front Ramp        | Sloped front hull panel, hazard stripes
Rear Ramp         | Rear slope, cargo hatch bulge
Side Ramp         | Angular side bulge, door panel
Elevator (Vertical)| Vertical hull panel, airlock hatch, reinforced struts
Elevator (Sub-Room)| Small hull protrusion, functional airlock detail
Snaps to grid based on bay node or deck offset

Orientation determines slope direction and panel placement

3️⃣ Drone / Fab / Rig Bays
Rule: These are child modules of belly bays or decks; they are physically in Fab, but visually represented on the exterior:

Interior Bay	Exterior Cue
Mobile Fab	Industrial vent stacks, paneling, crane supports
Drone Bay	Small launch ports, antennae, panel hatches
Player Rig Bay	Hull indentation, docking clamps, armor access hatch
Rover / Grav Bay	Hull bulge with ramp door, docking rails, mag-lock points
Procedural Rule: Each bay automatically generates proxy hull geometry for exterior recognition, snapped to deck/grid, maintaining low-poly readability.

4️⃣ Hull Panel / Vent / Industrial Accents
Rule: Hull panels and accents are semi-procedural decorations applied after primary hull is generated:

Panel Sizes: Match module size (e.g., fab panel = 3x2 polys, drone port = 1x1 polys)

Vents: Place on hull surfaces adjacent to functional interior nodes (fab, engine, drone bay)

Industrial Accents: Struts, pipes, antennas, hazard stripes — optional for visual clarity, always low-poly

Procedural Application Algorithm:

for each HullFace in ExteriorHull:
    if HullFace adjacent to InteriorModule:
        if Module.type == Fab:
            AddPanels(HullFace, pattern="industrial", color="orange/gray")
            AddVents(HullFace, count=2)
        if Module.type == DroneBay:
            AddSmallHatch(HullFace)
            AddAntenna(HullFace)
        if Module.type == Elevator:
            AddVerticalReinforcedPanels(HullFace)
Notes:

Panels and vents are purely visual cues, do not affect collision or gameplay unless intended.

Keeps Surrounded low-poly style readable, functional, and industrial.

1️⃣ Core Principles: Hull “Wrap” Around Interior Modules
Module-to-Mesh Mapping

Every interior module (bay, rig, fab, drone node, room) is a volume block.

Hull mesh stretches and interpolates around these blocks, maintaining a readable silhouette.

Hull polygons are low-poly convex approximations of interior volumes.

Hull Filling

Gaps between modules are automatically filled:

Between decks: vertical hull panels or connecting struts

Between side / rear offsets: hull extensions / bridging polygons

Between bays: angled panels to maintain industrial aesthetic

Mesh Stretching

Hull mesh can bend / taper slightly to integrate modules while keeping modular cues readable

Exterior hull respects module orientation and preserves ramp/elevator slope

2️⃣ Hallway & Filler Room Logic
Hallways

Procedurally generate corridors between interior modules if:

Modules are on same deck or offset decks with aligned connection points

Hallway nodes have prefabricated geometry templates:

Length = distance between modules

Width = minimum player / vehicle clearance

Optional support beams / vents along sides

Filler Rooms

Randomly placed in gaps or unused volumes for:

Aesthetic variety (control rooms, storage, small rooms)

Gameplay function (cargo container placement, minor systems)

Each filler room snaps to parent grid and contributes convex hull to exterior

Prefixed templates ensure:

Consistent scale

Surrounded aesthetic

Readable low-poly shape

3️⃣ Procedural Mesh Generation Algorithm
struct InteriorModule
{
    Vector3 position;
    Vector3 size; // bounds
    ModuleType type;
    vector<InteriorModule*> children;
};

struct HullMesh
{
    vector<Vector3> vertices;
    vector<int> indices;
};

HullMesh GenerateHull(vector<InteriorModule*>& modules)
{
    HullMesh hull;

    // Step 1: Wrap modules
    for (auto& m : modules)
    {
        // Generate convex hull around each module
        HullMesh moduleHull = GenerateModuleHull(m);
        MergeHull(hull, moduleHull);
    }

    // Step 2: Fill gaps
    for (auto& gap : FindGapsBetweenModules(modules))
    {
        HullMesh filler = GenerateFillerGeometry(gap);
        MergeHull(hull, filler);
    }

    // Step 3: Hallway generation
    for (auto& pair : FindModulePairsForHallways(modules))
    {
        HullMesh hallway = GenerateHallwayMesh(pair.first, pair.second);
        MergeHull(hull, hallway);
    }

    // Step 4: Stretch / interpolate hull to create smooth exterior
    hull = StretchHullAroundModules(hull, modules);

    // Step 5: Apply Surrounded low-poly aesthetic (triangles, paneling)
    hull = ApplyLowPolyStyling(hull);

    return hull;
}
4️⃣ Modular Rules for Larger Ships (Frigate+)

Prefabricated filler rooms:

Cargo rooms, storage, engine tunnels

Optional aesthetic-only modules (vents, structural struts)

Recursive snapping: each child module (hallway, filler, bay) automatically contributes to hull convex volume

5️⃣ Player / Vehicle Interaction Mapping

Cargo / Storage

Filler rooms provide logical locations for in-game items

Hull sections around these rooms visually show storage bays without breaking silhouette

{

    for (auto& m : modules)

        HullMesh moduleHull = GenerateModuleHull(m);
        MergeHull(hull, moduleHull);

3️⃣ Recursive Procedural Generation Pseudo-Code
struct Module {
    string name;
    ModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Vector3 position;
    vector<Module*> children;
    vector<Module> installedModules;
    VehicleClass allowedClass; // for bays
    Stats CalculateStats() {
        Stats s = baseStats[type];
        for(auto& m : installedModules) s += m.bonuses;
        return s;
    }
};

// Merge convex hulls from child modules into parent
HullMesh MergeHull(HullMesh parent, HullMesh child);

// Stretch hull around modules for smooth exterior
HullMesh StretchHullAroundModules(HullMesh hull, vector<Module*>& modules);

// Procedural low-poly styling
HullMesh ApplyLowPolyStyling(HullMesh hull);

HullMesh GenerateHull(vector<Module*>& modules)
{
    HullMesh hull;
    for(auto& m : modules) {
        HullMesh moduleHull = GenerateModuleHull(m);
        MergeHull(hull, moduleHull);
    }
    for(auto& gap : FindGaps(modules)) {
        HullMesh filler = GenerateFillerGeometry(gap);
        MergeHull(hull, filler);
    }
    for(auto& pair : FindModulePairsForHallways(modules)) {
        HullMesh hallway = GenerateHallwayMesh(pair.first, pair.second);
        MergeHull(hull, hallway);
    }
    hull = StretchHullAroundModules(hull, modules);
    hull = ApplyLowPolyStyling(hull);
    return hull;
}

// Recursive node expansion
void ExpandNode(Module* node) {
    for(auto& child : node->children) {
        SnapModuleToGrid(*child, *node); // Align child to parent
        ExpandNode(child);
    }
}

3️⃣ Skeleton Code for NovaForge Integration
// LandingSystem.h
struct LandingSite {
    Vector3 position;
    float slope;
    bool isFlat;
};

class LandingSystem
{
public:
    // Find flat landing site within target area
    LandingSite FindFlatLandingSite(Vector3 planetCenter, float radius, Ship& ship);

    // Align ship to terrain
    void AlignShipToTerrain(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site);

    // Deploy vehicles from belly bay
    void DeployRoversAndGravBikes(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site);
};

// LandingSystem.cpp
LandingSite LandingSystem::FindFlatLandingSite(Vector3 planetCenter, float radius, Ship& ship)
{
    vector<LandingSite> candidates;
    for(int i=0; i<MAX_SAMPLES; i++)
    {
        Vector3 sample = RandomPointInRadius(planetCenter, radius);
        float slope = SampleLocalSlope(sample, ship.GetFootprint());
        if(slope <= ship.maxLandingSlope)
            candidates.push_back({sample, slope, true});
    }
    // Pick candidate with largest contiguous flat area
    return SelectBestCandidate(candidates);
}

void LandingSystem::AlignShipToTerrain(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site)
{
    ship.position = site.position;
    ship.rotation = ComputeTiltCompensation(site.slope, ship.forwardVector);
}

void LandingSystem::DeployRoversAndGravBikes(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site)
{
    for(auto& vehicle : ship.bellyBay.vehicles)
    {
        Vector3 spawnPos = ComputeRampExitPosition(ship, vehicle);
        vehicle.SpawnAt(spawnPos, site);
    }
}

Deployment sequence is deterministic:

[Player chooses landing location OR system picks seed-based location]
   ↓
[Check local terrain heightmap]
   ├─ Determine ship footprint & max landing slope
   ├─ Sample local heights
   └─ Flatten region: adjust terrain vertices to target elevation

   ├─ Terrain, rocks, vegetation, features generated around landing site
   └─ Ensure procedural continuity
[Ship lands]
   ├─ Align belly bay / ramps
   └─ Deploy vehicles / drones / rigs
2️⃣ Pseudo-Code Skeleton
// ProceduralLandingSite.h
struct LandingSite {
    Vector3 position;      // Center of landing
    Vector3 size;          // Footprint (x/z)
    float targetHeight;    // Flattened elevation
    bool isCreated;        // Flag to know if site was generated
};

class ProceduralLandingSiteGenerator
{
public:
    LandingSite CreateFlatSite(Vector3 requestedPosition, Vector3 shipFootprint, Planet& planet);
    void FlattenTerrain(LandingSite& site, Planet& planet);
    void ReserveArea(LandingSite& site, Planet& planet);
};
// ProceduralLandingSite.cpp
LandingSite ProceduralLandingSiteGenerator::CreateFlatSite(Vector3 requestedPosition, Vector3 shipFootprint, Planet& planet)
{
    LandingSite site;
    site.position = requestedPosition;

    // Sample terrain under footprint
    float avgHeight = planet.SampleAverageHeight(requestedPosition, shipFootprint);
    site.targetHeight = avgHeight;

    // Flatten terrain locally
    FlattenTerrain(site, planet);

    // Reserve area to avoid procedural collisions
    ReserveArea(site, planet);

    site.size = shipFootprint;
    site.isCreated = true;
    return site;
}

void ProceduralLandingSiteGenerator::FlattenTerrain(LandingSite& site, Planet& planet)
{
    // Get all terrain vertices within ship footprint
    auto vertices = planet.GetVerticesInArea(site.position, site.size);

    // Adjust each vertex height toward targetHeight
    for(auto& v : vertices) {
        v.y = site.targetHeight;
    }

    // Optional: smooth edges with surrounding terrain
    planet.SmoothEdgesAround(site.position, site.size);
}

void ProceduralLandingSiteGenerator::ReserveArea(LandingSite& site, Planet& planet)
{
    planet.MarkReserved(site.position, site.size);
}
3️⃣ Integration with Ship & Deployment System
LandingSite site = landingSiteGenerator.CreateFlatSite(playerRequestedPos, ship.GetFootprint(), currentPlanet);

// Align ship with site
landingSystem.AlignShipToTerrain(ship, site);

// Deploy belly bay modules
landingSystem.DeployRoversAndGravBikes(ship, site);

// Resume planet generation normally around landing site
planet.GenerateFeaturesAround(site);

struct Module {
    string name;
    ModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Vector3 position;
    vector<Module*> children;
    vector<Module> installedModules;
    Stats CalculateStats();
};

void ExpandNode(Module* node) {
    for(auto& child : node->children) {
        SnapModuleToGrid(*child, *node);
        ExpandNode(child); // recursive expansion
    }
}

HullMesh GenerateHull(vector<Module*>& modules) {
    HullMesh hull;
    for(auto& m : modules) {
        HullMesh moduleHull = GenerateModuleHull(m);
        MergeHull(hull, moduleHull);
    }
    for(auto& gap : FindGaps(modules)) {
        MergeHull(hull, GenerateFillerGeometry(gap));
    }
    for(auto& pair : FindModulePairsForHallways(modules)) {
        MergeHull(hull, GenerateHallwayMesh(pair.first, pair.second));
    }
    hull = StretchHullAroundModules(hull, modules);
    return ApplyLowPolyStyling(hull);
}
Hull wraps all interior modules (multi-deck offsets supported)

Stats from modules propagate to all child nodes (vehicles, drones, rigs)

NovaForge Procedural Ship & Planetary Landing Skeleton
// ===============================
// Module Definitions
// ===============================
enum ModuleType {
    Deck,
    BellyBay,
    Rover,
    GravBike,
    MobileFab,
    DroneBay,
    PlayerRig,
    Hallway,
    FillerRoom
};

struct Stats {
    float power;
    float defense;
    float speed;
    // extend with modular stats
};

struct Module {
    string name;
    ModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;          // Dimensions
    Vector3 position;      // Local to parent
    vector<Module*> children;
    vector<Module> installedModules; // e.g., Fab modules, drone modules
    Stats CalculateStats() {
        Stats s{};
        for(auto& m : installedModules) s += m.bonuses;
        return s;
    }
};

// ===============================
// Hull Generation
// ===============================
struct HullMesh {
    // store vertices, triangles, color/industrial accents
};

HullMesh GenerateModuleHull(Module& m);
HullMesh MergeHull(HullMesh parent, HullMesh child);
HullMesh StretchHullAroundModules(HullMesh hull, vector<Module*>& modules);
HullMesh ApplyLowPolyStyling(HullMesh hull);

HullMesh GenerateHull(vector<Module*>& modules) {
    HullMesh hull;
    for(auto& m : modules) {
        HullMesh moduleHull = GenerateModuleHull(m);
        MergeHull(hull, moduleHull);
    }
    for(auto& gap : FindGaps(modules)) {
        HullMesh filler = GenerateFillerGeometry(gap);
        MergeHull(hull, filler);
    }
    for(auto& pair : FindModulePairsForHallways(modules)) {
        HullMesh hallway = GenerateHallwayMesh(pair.first, pair.second);
        MergeHull(hull, hallway);
    }
    hull = StretchHullAroundModules(hull, modules);
    return ApplyLowPolyStyling(hull);
}

// ===============================
// Recursive Node Expansion
// ===============================
void ExpandNode(Module* node) {
    for(auto& child : node->children) {
        SnapModuleToGrid(*child, *node);
        ExpandNode(child);
    }
}

// ===============================
// Vehicle / Drone / Rig Deployment
// ===============================
struct Vehicle { Vector3 position; ModuleType type; Stats stats; void SpawnAt(Vector3 pos); };
struct Drone { Vector3 position; ModuleType type; Stats stats; void DeployAt(Vector3 pos); };
struct PlayerRig { Vector3 position; Stats stats; };

struct BellyBay {
    vector<Vehicle> vehicles;
    ModuleType bayType; // Rover / GravBike / Fab
};

struct DroneBay {
    vector<Drone> drones;
};

struct Ship {
    Vector3 position;
    Vector3 rotation;
    Module rootModule;
    HullMesh hull;
    BellyBay bellyBay;
    DroneBay droneBay;
    PlayerRig playerRig;
    Vector3 GetFootprint();
    float maxLandingSlope;
};

// ===============================
// Planetary Landing System
// ===============================
struct LandingSite {
    Vector3 position;
    Vector3 size;      // Footprint of ship
    float targetHeight; 
    bool isCreated;
};

class LandingSystem {
public:
    LandingSite CreateFlatSite(Vector3 requestedPosition, Ship& ship, Planet& planet);
    void FlattenTerrain(LandingSite& site, Planet& planet);
    void AlignShipToTerrain(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site);
    void DeployVehiclesAndRigs(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site);
};

// ===============================
// Build / Upgrade / Deployment Queue
// ===============================
struct BuildTask { float timeRemaining; function<void()> onComplete; };

struct DeploymentQueue {
    queue<BuildTask> tasks;

    void AddTask(BuildTask task) { tasks.push(task); }
    void Update(float deltaTime) {
        if(!tasks.empty()) {
            tasks.front().timeRemaining -= deltaTime;
            if(tasks.front().timeRemaining <= 0.0f) {
                tasks.front().onComplete();
                tasks.pop();
            }
        }
    }
};

// ===============================
// Master Recursive Generation Pipeline
// ===============================
void GenerateShipRecursive(Ship& ship) {
    // 1. Expand interior modules recursively
    ExpandNode(&ship.rootModule);

    // 2. Generate hull around modules
    vector<Module*> modules = GatherAllModules(&ship.rootModule);
    ship.hull = GenerateHull(modules);

    // 3. Initialize vehicles, drones, rigs
    for(auto& v : ship.bellyBay.vehicles) {
        Vector3 spawnPos = ComputeRampExitPosition(ship, v);
        v.SpawnAt(spawnPos);
    }
    for(auto& d : ship.droneBay.drones) {
        Vector3 spawnPos = ComputeDroneBayPosition(ship, d);
        d.DeployAt(spawnPos);
    }
    // Player rig starts docked
    ship.playerRig.position = ComputePlayerRigPosition(ship);

    // 4. Planetary landing
    LandingSystem landing;
    LandingSite site = landing.CreateFlatSite(ship.position, ship, currentPlanet);
    landing.AlignShipToTerrain(ship, site);
    landing.DeployVehiclesAndRigs(ship, site);

    // 5. Build / upgrade / deployment queue handles timers
}

Flat-site creation ensures ships can land anywhere safely and deployment aligns with terrain.

Low-poly Surrounded style applied automatically by ApplyLowPolyStyling().

Modular stats propagate from interior modules → vehicles → drones → player rigs → tools.

Snap-to-grid editors and multi-deck offsets are compatible with this skeleton.

6️⃣ Complete Recursive PCG Ship & Landing Pipeline
void GenerateShipAndDeploy(Ship& ship, Planet& planet) {
    // 1. Expand ship interior recursively
    ExpandNode(&ship.rootModule);

    // 2. Generate hull
    vector<Module*> modules = GatherAllModules(&ship.rootModule);
    ship.hull = GenerateHull(modules);

    // 3. Initialize vehicles/drones/rig
    InitializeVehiclesAndDrones(ship);

    // 4. Create flat landing site
    LandingSite site = landingSystem.CreateFlatSite(ship.position, ship, planet);

    // 5. Align ship & deploy
    landingSystem.AlignShipToTerrain(ship, site);
    landingSystem.DeployVehiclesAndRigs(ship, site);

    // 6. Start build/upgrade queue
    for(auto& module : modules) {
        deploymentQueue.AddTask(BuildTask{
            .timeRemaining = ComputeBuildTime(module),
            .onComplete = [module]() { module.completed = true; }
        });
    }
}

1️⃣ Mesh Generation for Procedural Modules
All procedural modules (ship interiors, hulls, bays, vehicles, drones, rigs, weapons/tools) should generate meshes dynamically from node definitions. This removes the need for art and keeps everything deterministic.

Pseudo-Code Skeleton
struct Mesh {
    vector<Vector3> vertices;
    vector<Vector3> normals;
    vector<Vector2> uvs;
    vector<int> indices;
    Color color;       // for low-poly style
};

Mesh GenerateModuleMesh(Module& module) {
    Mesh mesh;

    // 1. Create primitive base shape for module
    mesh.vertices = CreateVerticesFromSize(module.size);
    mesh.indices  = GenerateTriangles(mesh.vertices);

    // 2. Add module-specific features (vents, panels, ramps, airlocks)
    if(module.type == ModuleType::BellyBay) {
        AddRamps(mesh, module);
        AddAirlock(mesh, module);
    }
    if(module.type == ModuleType::DroneBay) {
        AddDroneHolders(mesh, module);
    }
    if(module.type == ModuleType::Deck) {
        AddFloorPanels(mesh, module);
    }

    // 3. Apply Surrounded-style low-poly aesthetic
    ColorModule(mesh, module);
    ApplyFlatShading(mesh);

    return mesh;
}

Mesh MergeMeshes(Mesh a, Mesh b) {
    // Merge vertices/indices, offset b by position relative to a
    // Maintain low-poly style continuity
    ...
    return merged;
}
Recursive Hull Generation just calls GenerateModuleMesh for all child nodes and merges them.

2️⃣ Multi-Tool PCG System
Your multi-tool is now a procedural system itself. Every module is a function, weapon, or tool attachment.

Module-Based Multi-Tool Architecture
enum ToolModuleType {
    PowerCore,
    Barrel,
    Grip,
    Scope,
    EnergyCell,
    Attachment,  // e.g., mining head, hacking probe, shield emitter
};

struct ToolModule {
    ToolModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Stats stats;       // Damage, range, mining efficiency, hacking strength
};

struct MultiTool {
    vector<ToolModule> mainWeaponModules;
    vector<ToolModule> sideArmModules;
    vector<ToolModule> utilityModules; // PCG functions like mining, hacking, repair
    Mesh mesh;
    
    void GenerateMesh() {
        mesh = Mesh();
        for(auto& m : mainWeaponModules) mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, GenerateModuleMesh(m));
        for(auto& m : sideArmModules) mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, GenerateModuleMesh(m));
        for(auto& m : utilityModules) mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, GenerateModuleMesh(m));
        ApplyLowPolyStyling(mesh);
    }
};
Modules can swap in/out dynamically in-game or via PCG editor.

Stats are propagated from modules → tool.

Multi-tool now functions as weapon + PCG system (e.g., mining, hacking, scanning).

NovaForge Engine-Ready Skeleton
// ===============================
// MODULE DEFINITIONS
// ===============================
enum ModuleType {
    Deck,
    BellyBay,
    Rover,
    GravBike,
    MobileFab,
    DroneBay,
    PlayerRig,
    Hallway,
    FillerRoom,
    WeaponModule,
    MultiToolModule
};

struct Stats {
    float power;
    float defense;
    float speed;
    float efficiency; // For mining/hacking/crafting
};

struct Module {
    string name;
    ModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Vector3 position; // Local to parent
    vector<Module*> children;
    vector<Module> installedModules;
    Stats CalculateStats() {
        Stats s{};
        for(auto& m : installedModules) s += m.bonuses;
        return s;
    }
};

// ===============================
// MESH GENERATION
// ===============================
struct Mesh {
    vector<Vector3> vertices;
    vector<int> indices;
    vector<Vector3> normals;
    vector<Vector2> uvs;
    Color color;
};

Mesh GenerateModuleMesh(Module& m) {
    Mesh mesh = CreatePrimitiveMesh(m.size);

    // Add module-specific geometry
    switch(m.type){
        case BellyBay: AddRamps(mesh,m); AddAirlock(mesh,m); break;
        case DroneBay: AddDroneHolders(mesh,m); break;
        case Hallway: AddHallwayMesh(mesh,m); break;
        case Deck: AddFloorPanels(mesh,m); break;
        case WeaponModule: AddWeaponGeometry(mesh,m); break;
        case MultiToolModule: AddToolGeometry(mesh,m); break;
    }

    ApplyLowPolyStyling(mesh);
    return mesh;
}

Mesh MergeMeshes(Mesh a, Mesh b){
    // Merge vertices/indices with position offsets
    ...
    return merged;
}

Mesh GenerateHull(vector<Module*>& modules){
    Mesh hull;
    for(auto& m : modules){
        hull = MergeMeshes(hull, GenerateModuleMesh(*m));
    }
    for(auto& gap : FindGaps(modules)){
        hull = MergeMeshes(hull, GenerateFillerGeometry(gap));
    }
    for(auto& pair : FindModulePairsForHallways(modules)){
        hull = MergeMeshes(hull, GenerateHallwayMesh(pair.first, pair.second));
    }
    hull = StretchHullAroundModules(hull, modules);
    return hull;
}

// ===============================
// RECURSIVE MODULE EXPANSION
// ===============================
void ExpandNode(Module* node){
    for(auto& child : node->children){
        SnapModuleToGrid(*child,*node);
        ExpandNode(child);
    }
}

// ===============================
// VEHICLES, DRONES, RIGS
// ===============================
struct Vehicle{ Vector3 position; ModuleType type; Stats stats; void SpawnAt(Vector3 pos); };
struct Drone{ Vector3 position; ModuleType type; Stats stats; void DeployAt(Vector3 pos); };
struct PlayerRig{ Vector3 position; Stats stats; };

struct BellyBay{
    vector<Vehicle> vehicles;
    ModuleType bayType;
};

struct DroneBay{
    vector<Drone> drones;
};

struct Ship{
    Vector3 position;
    Vector3 rotation;
    Module rootModule;
    Mesh hull;
    BellyBay bellyBay;
    DroneBay droneBay;
    PlayerRig playerRig;
    Vector3 GetFootprint();
    float maxLandingSlope;
};

// ===============================
// PLANETARY LANDING SYSTEM
// ===============================
struct LandingSite{ Vector3 position; Vector3 size; float targetHeight; bool isCreated; };

class LandingSystem{
public:
    LandingSite CreateFlatSite(Vector3 requestedPosition, Ship& ship, Planet& planet);
    void FlattenTerrain(LandingSite& site, Planet& planet);
    void AlignShipToTerrain(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site);
    void DeployVehiclesAndRigs(Ship& ship, const LandingSite& site);
};

// ===============================
// BUILD / UPGRADE / DEPLOYMENT QUEUE
// ===============================
struct BuildTask{ float timeRemaining; function<void()> onComplete; };

struct DeploymentQueue{
    queue<BuildTask> tasks;
    void AddTask(BuildTask task){ tasks.push(task); }
    void Update(float deltaTime){
        if(!tasks.empty()){
            tasks.front().timeRemaining -= deltaTime;
            if(tasks.front().timeRemaining <= 0.0f){
                tasks.front().onComplete();
                tasks.pop();
            }
        }
    }
};

// ===============================
// MULTI-TOOL PCG SYSTEM
// ===============================
enum ToolModuleType{ PowerCore, Barrel, Grip, Scope, EnergyCell, Attachment };

struct ToolModule{
    ToolModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Stats stats;
};

struct MultiTool{
    vector<ToolModule> mainWeaponModules;
    vector<ToolModule> sideArmModules;
    vector<ToolModule> utilityModules; // mining, hacking, repair
    Mesh mesh;

    void GenerateMesh(){
        mesh = Mesh();
        for(auto& m : mainWeaponModules) mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, GenerateModuleMesh(m));
        for(auto& m : sideArmModules) mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, GenerateModuleMesh(m));
        for(auto& m : utilityModules) mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, GenerateModuleMesh(m));
        ApplyLowPolyStyling(mesh);
    }

    Stats CalculateStats(){
        Stats s{};
        for(auto& m : mainWeaponModules) s += m.stats;
        for(auto& m : sideArmModules) s += m.stats;
        for(auto& m : utilityModules) s += m.stats;
        return s;
    }
};

// ===============================
// MASTER PCG PIPELINE
// ===============================
void GenerateShipAndDeploy(Ship& ship, Planet& planet){
    // 1. Expand modules recursively
    ExpandNode(&ship.rootModule);

    // 2. Gather all modules for hull generation
    vector<Module*> modules = GatherAllModules(&ship.rootModule);
    ship.hull = GenerateHull(modules);

    // 3. Initialize vehicles, drones, rigs
    for(auto& v : ship.bellyBay.vehicles) v.SpawnAt(ComputeRampExitPosition(ship,v));
    for(auto& d : ship.droneBay.drones) d.DeployAt(ComputeDroneBayPosition(ship,d));
    ship.playerRig.position = ComputePlayerRigPosition(ship);

    // 4. Flat landing site
    LandingSystem landing;
    LandingSite site = landing.CreateFlatSite(ship.position, ship, planet);
    landing.AlignShipToTerrain(ship, site);
    landing.DeployVehiclesAndRigs(ship, site);

    // 5. Build/upgrade queue
    DeploymentQueue queue;
    for(auto& m : modules){
        queue.AddTask(BuildTask{
            .timeRemaining = ComputeBuildTime(*m),
            .onComplete = [m](){ m.completed = true; }
        });
    }
}

// ===============================
// NOTES
// ===============================
// - Fully recursive, seed-locked deterministic builds
// - Hull wrapping applies industrial low-poly Surrounded aesthetic
// - All interior/exterior modules, vehicles, drones, rigs, multi-tool modules share same PCG mesh system
// - Multi-tool doubles as modular PCG system and weapon/tool platform
// - Flat planetary landing integrated with procedural terrain

ChatGPT said:
Perfect — let’s do it. Here’s a text-based editor workflow skeleton for NovaForge that’s fully tied into the recursive PCG system, showing drag-and-drop modules, hull preview generation, ramp/elevator alignment, and multi-tool PCG function selection. This is fully engine-ready, no art required, and can be merged directly.

NovaForge PCG Editor Workflow Skeleton
// ===============================
// EDITOR MODULE DEFINITIONS
// ===============================
enum EditorMode {
    ShipModule,
    VehicleModule,
    DroneModule,
    PlayerRigModule,
    MultiToolModule
};

struct EditorSlot {
    Module* module;         // The module being edited/placed
    Vector3 gridPosition;   // Snap-to-grid location
    EditorMode mode;        // Current editing mode
};

// ===============================
// EDITOR WORKFLOW
// ===============================
class PCGEditor {
public:
    Ship* currentShip;
    MultiTool* currentTool;
    EditorMode activeMode;
    Module* selectedModule;
    Mesh previewMesh;

    void EnterEditor(Ship* ship, MultiTool* tool){
        currentShip = ship;
        currentTool = tool;
        activeMode = ShipModule;
        GeneratePreview();
    }

    void SelectModule(Module* module){
        selectedModule = module;
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void SetMode(EditorMode mode){
        activeMode = mode;
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void DragModuleTo(Vector3 position){
        if(!selectedModule) return;
        selectedModule->position = SnapToGrid(position);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void SnapModule(Module* module){
        module->position = SnapToGrid(module->position);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void RotateModule(Module* module, float angle){
        module->rotation.y += angle;
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void UpdatePreview(){
        // Regenerate hull and module meshes for live preview
        vector<Module*> allModules = GatherAllModules(&currentShip->rootModule);
        previewMesh = GenerateHull(allModules);

        // Add multi-tool preview if active
        if(activeMode == MultiToolModule && currentTool){
            currentTool->GenerateMesh();
            previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, currentTool->mesh);
        }
    }

    Vector3 SnapToGrid(Vector3 pos){
        const float gridSize = 1.0f;
        return Vector3(
            round(pos.x / gridSize) * gridSize,
            round(pos.y / gridSize) * gridSize,
            round(pos.z / gridSize) * gridSize
        );
    }

    void PlaceModule(Module* module){
        currentShip->rootModule.children.push_back(module);
        ExpandNode(module);      // Expand recursively if it has children
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void RemoveModule(Module* module){
        auto& children = currentShip->rootModule.children;
        children.erase(remove(children.begin(), children.end(), module), children.end());
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    // Ramp / Elevator alignment
    void AlignRampOrElevator(Module* module){
        if(module->type != ModuleType::BellyBay) return;
        module->position = ComputeOptimalRampPosition(currentShip, module);
        module->rotation = ComputeOptimalRampRotation(currentShip, module);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    // Multi-tool PCG Function Selector
    void AssignToolFunction(ToolModule* toolModule, ToolModuleType functionType){
        toolModule->type = functionType;
        currentTool->GenerateMesh();
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    // Save current editor state
    void SaveEditorState(){
        // Export module positions, hull meshes, tool configs
        SaveShipState(currentShip);
        SaveToolState(currentTool);
    }
};

// ===============================
// EDITOR USAGE EXAMPLE
// ===============================
PCGEditor editor;
editor.EnterEditor(&playerShip, &playerTool);
editor.SetMode(EditorMode::ShipModule);

// Drag & drop a new Deck
Module* newDeck = CreateModule("Deck A", ModuleType::Deck, Vector3(4,1,4));
editor.SelectModule(newDeck);
editor.DragModuleTo(Vector3(0,0,0));
editor.PlaceModule(newDeck);

// Snap & align ramps
editor.AlignRampOrElevator(&playerShip.bellyBay.rootModule);

// Multi-tool PCG function swap
editor.SetMode(EditorMode::MultiToolModule);
editor.AssignToolFunction(&playerTool.utilityModules[0], ToolModuleType::MiningHead);

// Update live preview
editor.UpdatePreview();

// Save final configuration
editor.SaveEditorState();

Let’s design a PCG editor skeleton and workflow for planetary stations, habitats, and hangars, incorporating ships and rovers as build platforms, drones assisting construction, and drag-and-drop modular placement with hull previews and build queues — fully deterministic and seed-locked, ready for NovaForge.

NovaForge Planetary Base Editor Skeleton
// ===============================
// MODULE TYPES FOR PLANETARY BASES
// ===============================
enum BaseModuleType {
    CoreHub,
    LivingQuarters,
    Lab,
    Workshop,
    FabricationBay,
    ShipHangar,
    VehicleBay,   // Rover / Grav Bike storage
    DroneFabBay,
    Corridor,
    FillerRoom,
    DefenseModule
};

// ===============================
// PLANETARY MODULE STRUCT
// ===============================
struct BaseModule {
    string name;
    BaseModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Vector3 position;  // Local to parent module
    vector<BaseModule*> children;
    vector<Module> installedSystems; // NPC/automation systems, consoles, etc.
    Stats CalculateStats() {
        Stats s{};
        for(auto& m : installedSystems) s += m.bonuses;
        return s;
    }
};

// ===============================
// PLANETARY BASE STRUCT
// ===============================
struct PlanetaryBase {
    Vector3 position;
    BaseModule rootModule;
    Mesh hull;
    vector<Ship*> supportShips;
    vector<Vehicle*> rovers;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
};

// ===============================
// PLANETARY BASE EDITOR
// ===============================
class BaseEditor {
public:
    PlanetaryBase* currentBase;
    EditorMode activeMode;
    BaseModule* selectedModule;
    Mesh previewMesh;

    void EnterEditor(PlanetaryBase* base){
        currentBase = base;
        activeMode = EditorMode::ShipModule; // default, can change to Drone or Vehicle
        GeneratePreview();
    }

    void SelectModule(BaseModule* module){
        selectedModule = module;
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void SetMode(EditorMode mode){
        activeMode = mode;
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void DragModuleTo(Vector3 position){
        if(!selectedModule) return;
        selectedModule->position = SnapToGrid(position);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void SnapModule(BaseModule* module){
        module->position = SnapToGrid(module->position);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void PlaceModule(BaseModule* module){
        currentBase->rootModule.children.push_back(module);
        ExpandNode(module);  // recursive placement
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void RemoveModule(BaseModule* module){
        auto& children = currentBase->rootModule.children;
        children.erase(remove(children.begin(), children.end(), module), children.end());
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    Vector3 SnapToGrid(Vector3 pos){
        const float gridSize = 2.0f;
        return Vector3(
            round(pos.x / gridSize) * gridSize,
            round(pos.y / gridSize) * gridSize,
            round(pos.z / gridSize) * gridSize
        );
    }

    // Generate hull mesh from all modules
    void UpdatePreview(){
        vector<BaseModule*> allModules = GatherAllModules(&currentBase->rootModule);
        previewMesh = GenerateBaseHull(allModules); // similar to GenerateHull in ships

        // Add ships, rovers, drones in preview
        for(auto& ship : currentBase->supportShips) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, ship->hull);
        for(auto& rover : currentBase->rovers) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, GenerateModuleMesh(rover));
        for(auto& drone : currentBase->drones) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, GenerateModuleMesh(drone));
    }

    // Assign ships/rovers to assist in building
    void AssignSupportUnit(Ship* ship){
        currentBase->supportShips.push_back(ship);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void AssignRover(Vehicle* rover){
        currentBase->rovers.push_back(rover);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void AssignDrone(Drone* drone){
        currentBase->drones.push_back(drone);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    // Build queue for modules + support assistance
    void AddBuildTask(BaseModule* module, float buildTime){
        BuildTask task{
            .timeRemaining = buildTime,
            .onComplete = [this,module](){
                module->installedSystems.push_back(Module{.name="Built", .type=ModuleType::Deck});
                UpdatePreview();
            }
        };
        deploymentQueue.AddTask(task);
    }

private:
    DeploymentQueue deploymentQueue;
};

// ===============================
// PLANETARY BASE GENERATION LOGIC
// ===============================
void GeneratePlanetaryBase(PlanetaryBase& base){
    ExpandNode(&base.rootModule);
    vector<BaseModule*> modules = GatherAllModules(&base.rootModule);
    base.hull = GenerateBaseHull(modules);
}

// ===============================
// SUPPORT SHIP / ROVER BUILD ASSIST
// ===============================
void ShipAssistConstruction(Ship& ship, PlanetaryBase& base){
    // Ship docks at base hangar
    // Drones deploy automatically to modules in build queue
    for(auto& drone : ship.droneBay.drones){
        drone.DeployAt(base.rootModule.position + Vector3(rand(),0,rand()));
        // Apply build contribution per drone type
    }
}

void RoverAssistConstruction(Vehicle& rover, PlanetaryBase& base){
    // Rover moves to module needing build
    // Activates fabrication bay for module assembly
}

// ===============================
// USAGE EXAMPLE
// ===============================
PlanetaryBase base;
BaseEditor editor;
editor.EnterEditor(&base);

// Place Core Hub
BaseModule* coreHub = new BaseModule{"Core Hub", BaseModuleType::CoreHub, Vector3(10,6,10)};
editor.SelectModule(coreHub);
editor.DragModuleTo(Vector3(0,0,0));
editor.PlaceModule(coreHub);

// Add Hangar and assign support ship
BaseModule* hangar = new BaseModule{"Ship Hangar", BaseModuleType::ShipHangar, Vector3(12,8,12)};
editor.PlaceModule(hangar);
Ship* supportShip = &playerShip;
editor.AssignSupportUnit(supportShip);

// Add Rover Bay and assign rover
BaseModule* roverBay = new BaseModule{"Rover Bay", BaseModuleType::VehicleBay, Vector3(6,4,10)};
editor.PlaceModule(roverBay);
editor.AssignRover(&playerRover);

// Drones assist in construction
Drone* buildDrone = new Drone();
editor.AssignDrone(buildDrone);

// Build queue for modules
editor.AddBuildTask(coreHub, 120.0f);    // 2 minutes
editor.AddBuildTask(hangar, 90.0f);
editor.AddBuildTask(roverBay, 60.0f);

// Live preview updates automatically
editor.UpdatePreview();

NovaForge Procedural Master Pipeline (Text Diagram)
[Planetary Base / Ship Landing Zone]
        │
        │ Procedural flat site detection
        │
        ▼
[Ship Arrival & Docking]
        │
        │ Assign docking node & belly bay alignment
        │ Initialize support ships, rovers, drones
        ▼
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                 SHIP SYSTEMS                     |
|  Ship Root Module (Frigate / Shuttle)            |
|   ├─ Belly Bay                                    |
|   │    ├─ Rover Slot                              |
|   │    │     ├─ Upgrade Modules                   |
|   │    │     └─ Build / Deployment Queue         |
|   │    ├─ Grav Bike Slot                           |
|   │    │     ├─ Elevator / Airlock                |
|   │    │     └─ Upgrade Modules                   |
|   │    ├─ Mobile Fabricator                         |
|   │    │     ├─ Drone Hull Assembly               |
|   │    │     └─ Component Production              |
|   │    └─ Ramp / Hull Integration                 |
|   ├─ Hull Wrapping & Low-Poly Surrounded Styling |
|   └─ Recursive Deck Expansion                     |
+---------------------------------------------------+
        │
        │ Recursive Module Expansion
        │ Hull mesh generation (live preview)
        ▼
[Player Rig / Suit System]
        │
        ├─ Rig Slot Modules (Defense, Recon, Healing, Shield)
        ├─ Rig Drones (up to 4 configurable)
        └─ Multi-Tool PCG Modules

NovaForge Procedural Pipeline Skeleton (C++ / Pseudo-Code)
// ===============================
// MODULE TYPES
// ===============================
enum ModuleType {
    ShipDeck,
    BellyBay,
    RoverSlot,
    GravBikeSlot,
    MobileFab,
    DroneBay,
    RigSlot,
    Corridor,
    FillerRoom,
    CoreHub,
    Hangar,
    LivingQuarters,
    Lab,
    Workshop,
    FabricationBay,
    DefenseModule
};

// ===============================
// BASE MODULE STRUCT
// ===============================
struct Module {
    string name;
    ModuleType type;
    Vector3 size;
    Vector3 position;         // Local relative to parent
    Quaternion rotation;
    vector<Module*> children;
    vector<Module*> dependencies;  // Modules that must complete before building
    vector<Module*> attachedSystems; // Multi-tool, drones, rigs, vehicles
    Stats moduleStats;

    bool IsBuildable() {
        for(auto dep : dependencies)
            if(!dep->built) return false;
        return true;
    }

    bool built = false;
};

// ===============================
// ENTITY DEFINITIONS
// ===============================
struct Vehicle {
    string name;
    Vector3 size;
    Module* assignedSlot;
    vector<Module*> modules;
    Mesh mesh;
    void Deploy(Vector3 targetPosition);
};

struct Drone {
    string name;
    Vector3 size;
    void AssistBuild(Module* targetModule);
    Mesh mesh;
};

struct Rig {
    string name;
    vector<Module*> slots;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Mesh mesh;
};

struct Ship {
    string name;
    Module rootModule;
    vector<Vehicle*> rovers;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Rig* playerRig;
    Mesh hull;
};

struct PlanetaryBase {
    string name;
    Module rootModule;
    vector<Ship*> supportShips;
    vector<Vehicle*> rovers;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Mesh hull;
};

// ===============================
// BUILD / DEPLOYMENT QUEUE
// ===============================
struct BuildTask {
    Module* targetModule;
    float timeRemaining;   // seconds
    function<void()> onComplete;
};

class BuildQueue {
    queue<BuildTask> tasks;
public:
    void AddTask(BuildTask task) { tasks.push(task); }
    void Update(float deltaTime) {
        if(tasks.empty()) return;
        BuildTask& task = tasks.front();
        task.timeRemaining -= deltaTime;
        if(task.timeRemaining <= 0) {
            task.targetModule->built = true;
            if(task.onComplete) task.onComplete();
            tasks.pop();
        }
    }
};

// ===============================
// PROCEDURAL NODE EXPANSION
// ===============================
void ExpandModule(Module* module) {
    // Recursively expand child modules if needed
    for(auto* child : module->children){
        if(!child->built) ExpandModule(child);
    }
}

// ===============================
// HULL GENERATION
// ===============================
Mesh GenerateHull(Module* rootModule) {
    vector<Module*> allModules = GatherAllModules(rootModule);
    Mesh hullMesh;
    for(auto* mod : allModules){
        hullMesh = MergeMeshes(hullMesh, GenerateModuleMesh(mod));
    }
    ApplyLowPolyStyling(hullMesh); // Surrounded aesthetic
    return hullMesh;
}

// ===============================
// PLANETARY FLAT SITE
// ===============================
Vector3 GenerateFlatLandingSite(Vector3 planetCoords, float radius) {
    // Sample terrain, flatten area if necessary
    Vector3 flatPosition = TerrainFlatten(planetCoords, radius);
    return flatPosition;
}

// ===============================
// SUPPORT UNITS
// ===============================
void AssignShipSupport(Ship* supportShip, PlanetaryBase* base) {
    base->supportShips.push_back(supportShip);
}

void AssignRoverSupport(Vehicle* rover, PlanetaryBase* base) {
    base->rovers.push_back(rover);
}

void DeployDrones(vector<Drone*>& drones, Module* targetModule) {
    for(auto& drone : drones){
        drone->AssistBuild(targetModule);
    }
}

// ===============================
// PLANETARY BASE / SHIP EDITOR
// ===============================
class PCGEditor {
public:
    Ship* activeShip;
    PlanetaryBase* activeBase;
    Module* selectedModule;
    BuildQueue buildQueue;
    Mesh previewMesh;

    void EnterShipEditor(Ship* ship) { activeShip = ship; UpdatePreview(); }
    void EnterBaseEditor(PlanetaryBase* base) { activeBase = base; UpdatePreview(); }

    void SelectModule(Module* module) { selectedModule = module; UpdatePreview(); }

    void DragModuleTo(Vector3 pos) { if(selectedModule){ selectedModule->position = SnapToGrid(pos); UpdatePreview(); } }

    void PlaceModule(Module* module){
        if(activeShip) activeShip->rootModule.children.push_back(module);
        else if(activeBase) activeBase->rootModule.children.push_back(module);
        ExpandModule(module);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void RemoveModule(Module* module){
        auto& children = activeShip ? activeShip->rootModule.children : activeBase->rootModule.children;
        children.erase(remove(children.begin(), children.end(), module), children.end());
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    Vector3 SnapToGrid(Vector3 pos){ float gridSize = 1.0f; return Vector3(round(pos.x/gridSize)*gridSize, round(pos.y/gridSize)*gridSize, round(pos.z/gridSize)*gridSize); }

    void AddBuildTask(Module* module, float buildTime){
        BuildTask task{module, buildTime, [this,module](){ module->built = true; UpdatePreview(); }};
        buildQueue.AddTask(task);
    }

    void UpdatePreview(){
        Module* root = activeShip ? &activeShip->rootModule : &activeBase->rootModule;
        previewMesh = GenerateHull(root);

        // Merge vehicles, drones, rigs meshes
        if(activeShip){
            for(auto& v : activeShip->rovers) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, v->mesh);
            for(auto& d : activeShip->drones) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, d->mesh);
            if(activeShip->playerRig) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, activeShip->playerRig->mesh);
        }
        if(activeBase){
            for(auto& s : activeBase->supportShips) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, s->hull);
            for(auto& v : activeBase->rovers) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, v->mesh);
            for(auto& d : activeBase->drones) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, d->mesh);
        }
    }
};

2️⃣ Ship Star Rating System
Ships are rated 1–5 stars, dynamically calculated from:

Installed modules (higher-tier modules increase rating)

Player skills (Engineering, Fabrication, Piloting)

Module synergy / support (e.g., drones or rigs increase effectiveness)

Module placement / optimization (centralized core hub = better rating)

Economic factors (planetary base resources, station proximity)

Example formula (pseudo-code):

int CalculateShipStarRating(Ship* ship, Player* player, PlanetaryBase* base) {
    float score = 0.0f;

    // Module contribution
    for(auto& mod : GatherAllModules(&ship->rootModule)){
        score += mod->tier * 2.0f;
    }

    // Player skill impact
    score += player->skills.engineering * 0.5f;
    score += player->skills.fabrication * 0.5f;
    score += player->skills.piloting * 0.2f;

    // Synergy bonuses (drones, rigs)
    score += ship->drones.size() * 1.0f;
    score += ship->playerRig ? 2.0f : 0.0f;

    // Module placement bonus (centralized cores)
    if(IsCentralizedCore(ship)) score += 2.0f;

    // Economic / planetary factor
    if(base && base->resources >= 5) score += 1.0f;

    // Clamp to 1-5
    int stars = std::min(5, std::max(1, int(round(score/5.0f))));
    return stars;
}
Visual cues by star rating:

Star	Hull / Module Visuals
1	Small, sparse, flat surfaces, minimal detail
2	Slight hull extensions, vents, small lights
3	Modular protrusions, visible machinery, more accent colors
4	Multi-level hull, ramps, visible conduits, bright lights
5	Full Surrounded aesthetic, industrial detailing, external machinery, decorative antennae, high-complexity hull wrapping
3️⃣ Module Upgrade Rules
Each module can be upgraded using:

Player resources (materials, credits)

Player skills (affects success / build time)

Supporting units (drones / rovers / ships)

Time-based progression (build queue system)

Example pseudo-code:

void UpgradeModule(Module* mod, Player* player, vector<Drone*> assistants){
    float baseTime = 60.0f; // seconds
    float skillModifier = 1.0f - player->skills.engineering*0.05f;
    float droneSpeed = 1.0f + assistants.size()*0.1f;
    float buildTime = baseTime * skillModifier / droneSpeed;

    BuildTask task;
    task.targetModule = mod;
    task.timeRemaining = buildTime;
    task.onComplete = [mod]() { mod->tier = std::min(5, mod->tier+1); };
    globalBuildQueue.AddTask(task);
}

Base modules influence the ship’s rating when docked or supported.

Planetary systems (flat landing sites, resources) feed into module efficiency and star rating.

System	Rating	Notes
Combat / Weapons	1–5	Turret upgrades, hull reinforcement, targeting computers
Mining / Salvage	1–5	Excavators, refinery modules, multi-tool synergy

2️⃣ Ship Data Structure Example
struct SystemRating {
    string systemName;       // e.g., "Combat"
    int tierRating;          // 1–5 stars
    float effectiveness;     // normalized 0.0–1.0
};

struct Ship {
    string name;
    Module rootModule;
    vector<SystemRating> systemRatings;
    vector<Vehicle*> rovers;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Rig* playerRig;
    Mesh hull;

    // Update all system ratings dynamically
    void UpdateSystemRatings(Player* player, PlanetaryBase* base) {
        systemRatings.clear();
        vector<string> systems = {"Combat","Mining","Fabrication","Exploration","Cargo","Defense"};

        for(auto& system : systems){
            int score = 0;
            float weight = 0.0f;

            for(auto* mod : GatherAllModules(&rootModule)){
                if(ModSupportsSystem(mod, system)){
                    score += mod->tier * 2;         // module tier contributes
                    weight += 1.0f;                 // normalize for multiple modules
                }
            }

            // Player / AI skill contribution
            score += player->GetSkillForSystem(system) * 0.5f;

            // Environment / planetary base impact
            if(base) score += BaseSupportsSystem(base, system) ? 1 : 0;

            int stars = std::min(5, std::max(1, int(round(score/5.0f))));
            systemRatings.push_back({system, stars, float(score)/10.0f});
        }
    }
};
3️⃣ AI Integration
AI ships can now make decisions based on system-specific ratings:

Example logic:

Ship* ChooseTarget(vector<Ship*>& enemies, string focusSystem){
    Ship* bestTarget = nullptr;
    int minRating = 999;
    for(auto* s : enemies){
        int systemStars = s->GetSystemRating(focusSystem);
        if(systemStars < minRating){ // prioritize weaker system
            minRating = systemStars;
            bestTarget = s;
        }
    }
    return bestTarget;
}
AI can also choose fleet composition, trading partners, or mission allocation based on system strengths:

Mining fleet → select ships with high Mining ratings

Combat fleet → prioritize high Combat/Defense ratings

Exploration → choose ships with high Sensors/Exploration ratings

Multi-system ships are more versatile but may be “jack-of-all-trades” if no system reaches 5 stars.

4️⃣ Implementation Notes
Ratings are dynamic: changing modules or upgrades automatically updates system ratings.

Weighted synergy: modules, drones, rigs, and player/AI skills contribute differently per system.

Persistent and deterministic: system ratings are seeded to allow reproducibility in procedural generation.

UI / player feedback: display multi-system ratings as star charts or bars per ship.

AI awareness: ratings directly influence tactical, economic, and support behaviors in-game.

This system now lets every ship, regardless of complexity, have nuanced stats per system, which propagates to AI decisions, player feedback, and procedural generation logic.

NovaForge Full Integrated Procedural Skeleton
// ===============================
// MODULE TYPES
// ===============================
enum ModuleType {
    ShipDeck,
    BellyBay,
    RoverSlot,
    GravBikeSlot,
    MobileFab,
    DroneBay,
    RigSlot,
    Corridor,
    FillerRoom,
    CoreHub,
    Hangar,
    LivingQuarters,
    Lab,
    Workshop,
    FabricationBay,
    DefenseModule
};

// ===============================
// BASE MODULE STRUCT
// ===============================
struct Module {
    string name;
    ModuleType type;
    int tier = 1;             // Upgrade tier 1-5
    Vector3 size;
    Vector3 position;
    Quaternion rotation;
    vector<Module*> children;
    vector<Module*> dependencies;
    vector<Module*> attachedSystems; // Vehicles, drones, rigs
    Stats moduleStats;
    bool built = false;

    bool IsBuildable() {
        for(auto dep : dependencies) if(!dep->built) return false;
        return true;
    }
};

// ===============================
// VEHICLES, DRONES, RIGS
// ===============================
struct Vehicle {
    string name;
    Vector3 size;
    Module* assignedSlot;
    vector<Module*> modules;
    Mesh mesh;
    void Deploy(Vector3 targetPosition);
};

struct Drone {
    string name;
    Vector3 size;
    void AssistBuild(Module* targetModule);
    Mesh mesh;
};

struct Rig {
    string name;
    vector<Module*> slots;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Mesh mesh;
};

// ===============================
// SYSTEM RATINGS
// ===============================
struct SystemRating {
    string systemName;   // e.g., "Combat", "Mining"
    int tierRating;      // 1-5 stars
    float effectiveness; // normalized 0.0-1.0
};

// ===============================
// SHIP STRUCTURE
// ===============================
struct Ship {
    string name;
    Module rootModule;
    vector<Vehicle*> rovers;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Rig* playerRig;
    Mesh hull;
    vector<SystemRating> systemRatings;

    void UpdateSystemRatings(Player* player, PlanetaryBase* base){
        systemRatings.clear();
        vector<string> systems = {"Combat","Mining","Fabrication","Exploration","Cargo","Defense"};

        for(auto& sys : systems){
            int score = 0;
            float weight = 0.0f;

            for(auto* mod : GatherAllModules(&rootModule)){
                if(ModSupportsSystem(mod, sys)){
                    score += mod->tier * 2;
                    weight += 1.0f;
                }
            }

            // Player skill impact
            score += player->GetSkillForSystem(sys) * 0.5f;

            // Base impact
            if(base && BaseSupportsSystem(base, sys)) score += 1;

            int stars = std::min(5, std::max(1, int(round(score/5.0f))));
            systemRatings.push_back({sys, stars, float(score)/10.0f});
        }
    }

    int GetSystemRating(string systemName){
        for(auto& r : systemRatings) if(r.systemName == systemName) return r.tierRating;
        return 1;
    }
};

// ===============================
// PLANETARY BASE
// ===============================
struct PlanetaryBase {
    string name;
    Module rootModule;
    vector<Ship*> supportShips;
    vector<Vehicle*> rovers;
    vector<Drone*> drones;
    Mesh hull;
    int resources;
};

// ===============================
// BUILD QUEUE
// ===============================
struct BuildTask {
    Module* targetModule;
    float timeRemaining;
    function<void()> onComplete;
};

class BuildQueue {
    queue<BuildTask> tasks;
public:
    void AddTask(BuildTask task){ tasks.push(task); }
    void Update(float deltaTime){
        if(tasks.empty()) return;
        BuildTask& task = tasks.front();
        task.timeRemaining -= deltaTime;
        if(task.timeRemaining <= 0){
            task.targetModule->built = true;
            if(task.onComplete) task.onComplete();
            tasks.pop();
        }
    }
};

// ===============================
// NODE EXPANSION
// ===============================
void ExpandModule(Module* module){
    for(auto* child : module->children)
        if(!child->built) ExpandModule(child);
}

// ===============================
// HULL GENERATION
// ===============================
Mesh GenerateHull(Module* rootModule){
    vector<Module*> allModules = GatherAllModules(rootModule);
    Mesh hullMesh;
    for(auto* mod : allModules){
        hullMesh = MergeMeshes(hullMesh, GenerateModuleMesh(mod));
    }
    ApplyLowPolyStyling(hullMesh); // Surrounded style
    return hullMesh;
}

// ===============================
// PLANETARY LANDING SITE
// ===============================
Vector3 GenerateFlatLandingSite(Vector3 planetCoords, float radius){
    return TerrainFlatten(planetCoords, radius);
}

// ===============================
// SUPPORT UNIT DEPLOYMENT
// ===============================
void AssignShipSupport(Ship* supportShip, PlanetaryBase* base){ base->supportShips.push_back(supportShip); }
void AssignRoverSupport(Vehicle* rover, PlanetaryBase* base){ base->rovers.push_back(rover); }
void DeployDrones(vector<Drone*>& drones, Module* targetModule){
    for(auto& drone : drones) drone->AssistBuild(targetModule);
}

// ===============================
// AI DECISION HOOKS
// ===============================
Ship* AIChooseTarget(vector<Ship*>& enemies, string focusSystem){
    Ship* bestTarget = nullptr;
    int minRating = 999;
    for(auto* s : enemies){
        int rating = s->GetSystemRating(focusSystem);
        if(rating < minRating){
            minRating = rating;
            bestTarget = s;
        }
    }
    return bestTarget;
}

// ===============================
// PCG EDITOR / MODULE INTERFACE
// ===============================
class PCGEditor {
public:
    Ship* activeShip;
    PlanetaryBase* activeBase;
    Module* selectedModule;
    BuildQueue buildQueue;
    Mesh previewMesh;

    void EnterShipEditor(Ship* ship){ activeShip = ship; UpdatePreview(); }
    void EnterBaseEditor(PlanetaryBase* base){ activeBase = base; UpdatePreview(); }

    void SelectModule(Module* module){ selectedModule = module; UpdatePreview(); }
    void DragModuleTo(Vector3 pos){ if(selectedModule){ selectedModule->position = SnapToGrid(pos); UpdatePreview(); } }

    void PlaceModule(Module* module){
        if(activeShip) activeShip->rootModule.children.push_back(module);
        else if(activeBase) activeBase->rootModule.children.push_back(module);
        ExpandModule(module);
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    void RemoveModule(Module* module){
        auto& children = activeShip ? activeShip->rootModule.children : activeBase->rootModule.children;
        children.erase(remove(children.begin(), children.end(), module), children.end());
        UpdatePreview();
    }

    Vector3 SnapToGrid(Vector3 pos){
        float gridSize = 1.0f;
        return Vector3(round(pos.x/gridSize)*gridSize,
                       round(pos.y/gridSize)*gridSize,
                       round(pos.z/gridSize)*gridSize);
    }

    void AddBuildTask(Module* module, float buildTime){
        BuildTask task{module, buildTime, [this,module](){ module->built=true; UpdatePreview(); }};
        buildQueue.AddTask(task);
    }

    void UpdatePreview(){
        Module* root = activeShip ? &activeShip->rootModule : &activeBase->rootModule;
        previewMesh = GenerateHull(root);
        if(activeShip){
            for(auto& v : activeShip->rovers) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, v->mesh);
            for(auto& d : activeShip->drones) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, d->mesh);
            if(activeShip->playerRig) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, activeShip->playerRig->mesh);
        }
        if(activeBase){
            for(auto& s : activeBase->supportShips) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, s->hull);
            for(auto& v : activeBase->rovers) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, v->mesh);
            for(auto& d : activeBase->drones) previewMesh = MergeMeshes(previewMesh, d->mesh);
        }
    }
};
✅ Features Implemented
Recursive procedural module expansion for ships, bays, planetary bases

Hull wrapping with Surrounded low-poly style

Belly bay → vehicles → drones → player rigs → mobile fabs propagation

Procedural flat planetary landing sites

Timed build & upgrade queue system

Multi-system star ratings per ship, affecting AI decisions

AI hooks to select targets based on system strengths/weaknesses

PCG editor skeleton for drag-and-drop module placement, snapping, and live preview

Perfect — let’s extend the NovaForge pipeline with procedural mesh generation, tiered visuals, multi-system star feedback, and recursive deployment simulation, all fully modular and code-driven. I’ll keep this engine-ready pseudo/C++ style for direct integration.

1️⃣ Procedural Mesh Generation
Each module generates a mesh procedurally, scaling and stretching to fit interior layout, hallways, bays, and corridors, maintaining the Surrounded low-poly aesthetic.

Mesh GenerateModuleMesh(Module* mod){
    Mesh mesh;

    // Base shape
    mesh = CreateBox(mod->size);

    // Hull deformation to fill gaps between connected modules
    for(auto* child : mod->children){
        Vector3 offset = child->position - mod->position;
        Mesh childMesh = GenerateModuleMesh(child);
        mesh = MergeMeshes(mesh, TranslateMesh(childMesh, offset));
    }

    // Tier-based details
    switch(mod->tier){
        case 2: AddPanels(mesh); break;
        case 3: AddVents(mesh); break;
        case 4: AddLights(mesh); break;
        case 5: AddComplexIndustrialAccents(mesh); break;
    }

    // Surrounded low-poly style simplification
    SimplifyMesh(mesh, targetPolygonCount=100 + mod->tier*50);

    return mesh;
}
Notes:

Modules automatically stretch/merge into hull shape.

Corridors/filler rooms can generate procedural props like crates or consoles for realism.

Mesh complexity scales with tier and module type.

2️⃣ Tier-Based Visual Updates
Tier-based visual cues for ships, bays, and stations:

void ApplyTierVisuals(Module* mod, Mesh& mesh){
    // Base materials
    mesh.material = GetBaseMaterial(mod->type);

    // Tier upgrades
    if(mod->tier >= 2) mesh.material = AddPanelTextures(mesh.material);
    if(mod->tier >= 3) mesh.material = AddVentsAndPipes(mesh.material);
    if(mod->tier >= 4) mesh.material = AddLightsAndAccents(mesh.material);
    if(mod->tier == 5) mesh.material = AddFullIndustrialAccents(mesh.material);
}
Visual feedback: exterior hull and interior reflect module upgrades.

Hull wrapping conforms to module expansions.

3️⃣ Player & AI Feedback UI
Multi-system star ratings are shown per ship or station:

void RenderSystemRatingUI(Ship* ship){
    for(auto& rating : ship->systemRatings){
        float filled = rating.tierRating / 5.0f;
        DrawStarBar(rating.systemName, filled);
    }
}

// AI reads these values for decisions
int GetSystemEffectiveness(Ship* ship, string system){
    for(auto& r : ship->systemRatings){
        if(r.systemName == system) return r.tierRating;
    }
    return 1;
}
UI displays stars per system (Combat, Mining, Fabrication, Exploration, Cargo, Defense).

AI uses the same ratings to choose targets, prioritize upgrades, or select missions.

4️⃣ Recursive Deployment Flow Simulation
All ship systems, drones, rigs, and planetary bases propagate recursively:

void DeployModuleRecursive(Module* mod){
    if(!mod->built) return;

    // Deploy attached vehicles/drones
    for(auto* v : mod->attachedSystems){
        if(auto* veh = dynamic_cast<Vehicle*>(v)) veh->Deploy(mod->position);
        else if(auto* d = dynamic_cast<Drone*>(v)) d->AssistBuild(mod);
    }

    // Expand child modules recursively
    for(auto* child : mod->children){
        DeployModuleRecursive(child);
    }

    // Update hull visuals dynamically
    Mesh updatedMesh = GenerateModuleMesh(mod);
    ApplyTierVisuals(mod, updatedMesh);
    mod->mesh = updatedMesh;
}
Supports multi-deck ships, ramp/elevator docking, and procedural bays.

Belly bays, rigs, mobile fabs, and drones propagate automatically.

Planetary bases can be deployed recursively with support ships and rovers.

Star Rating UI: Player sees multi-system ratings; AI reads them for tactical decisions.

Recursive Deployment: Ships, vehicles, drones, rigs, and planetary bases propagate automatically; hulls regenerate in real-time.

1️⃣ EXACT MODE CONTROLLER — CODE SKELETON (AUTHORITATIVE)
This is the single choke point for FPS ⇄ Flight ⇄ Fleet.

Core Types
enum class PlayerMode {
    FPS,
    FLIGHT,
    FLEET_COMMAND
};
Mode Interface (no cross-talk allowed)
class IPlayerMode {
public:
    virtual ~IPlayerMode() = default;

    virtual void OnEnter() = 0;
    virtual void OnExit() = 0;
    virtual void Tick(float dt) = 0;

    // hard ownership
    virtual void BindInput() = 0;
    virtual void UnbindInput() = 0;

    virtual void ActivateUI() = 0;
    virtual void DeactivateUI() = 0;

    virtual void ActivateCamera() = 0;
    virtual void DeactivateCamera() = 0;
};
PlayerModeController (this owns everything)
class PlayerModeController {
public:
    void RegisterMode(PlayerMode mode, std::unique_ptr<IPlayerMode> impl);
    void RequestMode(PlayerMode target);
    void Tick(float dt);

    PlayerMode GetCurrent() const { return current; }

private:
    PlayerMode current = PlayerMode::FPS;
    PlayerMode pending = PlayerMode::FPS;

    std::unordered_map<PlayerMode, std::unique_ptr<IPlayerMode>> modes;

    void Transition();
};
Transition Logic (NO SHORTCUTS)
void PlayerModeController::RequestMode(PlayerMode target) {
    if (target == current) return;
    pending = target;
}

void PlayerModeController::Tick(float dt) {
    if (pending != current) {
        Transition();
    }
    modes[current]->Tick(dt);
}

void PlayerModeController::Transition() {
    auto& from = modes[current];
    auto& to   = modes[pending];

    from->UnbindInput();
    from->DeactivateUI();
    from->DeactivateCamera();
    from->OnExit();

    // optional: fade / time-slow hook here

    to->OnEnter();
    to->ActivateCamera();
    to->ActivateUI();
    to->BindInput();

    current = pending;
}
Rule:
If something feels wrong → fix the transition, not the mode.

2️⃣ FLEET COMMAND UI — WIREFRAME & LANGUAGE (LOCKED)
Visual Identity
Holographic

Abstracted (no ship interiors)

Readable at a glance

Zero twitch actions

Screen Layout (Top-Down Tactical)
┌────────────────────────────────────┐
│   SYSTEM MAP (TACTICAL OVERLAY)     │
│                                    │
│   ○ Friendly Fleet                 │
│   △ Enemy Contacts                 │
│   ─ Vector / Formation Lines       │
│                                    │

Fleet Order Object (THIS IS YOUR RTS CORE)
enum class FleetIntent {
    ENGAGE,
    DEFEND,
    ESCORT,
    RETREAT,
    HOLD,
    REGROUP
};

struct FleetOrder {
    FleetIntent intent;
    EntityID target;          // enemy fleet, ally, or location proxy
    float aggression;         // 0.0 – 1.0
};
RTS mode never controls ships directly.
It issues intent → Fleet AI resolves.

RTS Mode Rules (Hard Lock)
Time scale: 0.15x

Weapons disabled

Thrusters disabled

Camera = tactical only

Exit RTS returns to exact prior flight state

Below is the minimum extra FPS layer that will make boarding feel finished instead of “tech demo”, without exploding scope.

🔑 FPS MUST DELIVER 4 FEELINGS
If these aren’t present, FPS will feel flat no matter how good the tech is:

Weight – movement, recoil, doors

Danger – damage, exposure, sound

Intent – player decisions matter

Context – this is a ship, not a hallway shooter

Everything below exists to serve those.

1️⃣ DAMAGE & SURVIVABILITY (CRITICAL)
Add a two-layer health model
struct Health {
    float shields;    // regen, absorbs first
    float suit;       // no regen in combat
};
Why this matters
Shields → aggressive play

Suit damage → panic, retreat, medkits

Makes boarding tense, not spongey

Add:

Suit breach warning (audio)

Screen frosting / vignette at low suit

2️⃣ MOVEMENT MODIFIERS BY ENVIRONMENT (BIG FEEL BOOST)
Boarding ships should feel different.

Add these states:
Normal gravity

Low gravity

Zero-G (EVA interior breaches)

Movement modifiers:

Reduced friction

Momentum carry

Wall push impulses

Even simple physics tweaks will sell the fantasy.

3️⃣ WEAPON FEEL (NOT VARIETY)
You do not need many guns.
You need 3 that feel distinct.

Minimum loadout
Weapon	Purpose
Rifle	Mid-range control
Shotgun	Breach / panic
Tool Cutter	Doors, weak points
Weapon feedback checklist
Camera kick

Shell ejection or energy vent

Audio echo in corridors

Hit sparks / decals

If it doesn’t sound good, it isn’t good.

4️⃣ AI BEHAVIOR (CHEAP BUT EFFECTIVE)
FPS AI doesn’t need to be smart — it needs to be legible.

Add just 3 behaviors:
Advance

Take cover

Fall back when hurt

Plus ONE rule:
Enemies retreat toward objectives, not randomly.

This creates natural flow and pushes player forward.

5️⃣ INTERACTION DENSITY (THIS SELLS “SHIP”)
FPS spaces need things to touch.

Add:

Manual doors (slow, loud)

Hack panels (short, risky)

Emergency lights

Breakable crates

Even fake interactions make spaces feel alive.

6️⃣ AUDIO IS NON-OPTIONAL
If you add only one thing, make it audio.

You need:
Footstep reverb (metal!)

Distant gunfire muffling

Breathing at low suit health

Door hydraulics

Alarm states

Audio does more immersion work than graphics ever will.

7️⃣ MINIMAL PROGRESSION (NO TREES)
FPS progression should be mission-scoped, not permanent (for now).

Add:

Temporary buffs

Salvaged weapon mods

One-use combat injectors

This avoids RPG bloat but gives choice.

8️⃣ ONE “OH SH*T” MOMENT (MANDATORY)
Every good FPS mission has one spike.

Examples:

Hull breach → zero-G combat

Lights out + emergency red

Reinforcements drop behind player

Script exactly one moment per mission.

That’s it. Don’t overdo it.

🚫 WHAT NOT TO ADD (YET)
❌ Skill trees
❌ Crafting benches
❌ NPC companions
❌ Complex stealth systems
❌ Dialogue trees

Those come later if the core feels good.

1️⃣ FPS COMBAT STATE MACHINE (PLAYER + ENEMY)
This keeps combat readable, debuggable, and cheap to iterate.

🎮 Player Combat States
enum class PlayerCombatState {
    EXPLORING,      // weapon lowered, traversal
    ALERT,          // enemy detected
    ENGAGED,        // active combat
    WOUNDED,        // suit damage, impaired
    BREACHED,       // zero-G / hull breach active
    DOWNED          // incapacitated
};
Transitions (authoritative):

EXPLORING → ALERT : enemy sight / sound

ALERT → ENGAGED : player fires or is fired upon

ENGAGED → WOUNDED : suit < 40%

ANY → BREACHED : hull breach event

WOUNDED → DOWNED : suit = 0

ENGAGED → EXPLORING : area clear

Rules

Movement speed −15% in WOUNDED

Breathing audio + vignette in WOUNDED

Aim sway increased in BREACHED

No healing during ENGAGED unless injector used

🤖 Enemy Combat States
enum class EnemyCombatState {
    IDLE,
    AWARE,
    ATTACKING,
    TAKING_COVER,
    RETREATING,
    DEAD
};
Key rule: enemies never teleport between states.
They move through space so players can read intent.

Gravity stabilizes

Player cannot die instantly

At least one enemy is killed by the breach

Player regains control quickly

1️⃣ FPS COMBAT STATE MACHINE — CODE
This is authoritative, tick-driven, and event-fed.

Player Combat State Component
enum class PlayerCombatState {
    EXPLORING,
    ALERT,
    ENGAGED,
    WOUNDED,
    BREACHED,
    DOWNED
};

struct PlayerCombatStateComponent {
    PlayerCombatState state = PlayerCombatState::EXPLORING;
    float suitHealth = 100.f;
    float shield = 100.f;
};
Combat State Update System
class PlayerCombatStateSystem {
public:
    void Tick(Entity player, float dt) {
        auto& combat = ecs.Get<PlayerCombatStateComponent>(player);

        switch (combat.state) {
            case PlayerCombatState::EXPLORING:
                if (EnemyDetected(player))
                    Transition(player, PlayerCombatState::ALERT);
                break;

            case PlayerCombatState::ALERT:
                if (PlayerFired(player) || TookDamage(player))
                    Transition(player, PlayerCombatState::ENGAGED);
                break;

            case PlayerCombatState::ENGAGED:
                if (combat.suitHealth < 40.f)
                    Transition(player, PlayerCombatState::WOUNDED);
                if (NoEnemiesNearby())
                    Transition(player, PlayerCombatState::EXPLORING);
                break;

            case PlayerCombatState::WOUNDED:
                ApplyMovementPenalty(player);
                if (combat.suitHealth <= 0.f)
                    Transition(player, PlayerCombatState::DOWNED);
                break;

            case PlayerCombatState::BREACHED:
                ApplyZeroGModifiers(player);
                break;

            case PlayerCombatState::DOWNED:
                DisableInput(player);
                break;
        }
    }

private:
    void Transition(Entity player, PlayerCombatState next) {
        auto& combat = ecs.Get<PlayerCombatStateComponent>(player);
        combat.state = next;
        EventBus::Emit(PlayerCombatStateChanged{player, next});
    }
};
✔ Centralized
✔ Debuggable
✔ Deterministic

2️⃣ HULL BREACH — REUSABLE EVENT SYSTEM
This is not scripted garbage — it’s a reusable environmental event.

Hull Breach Event Definition
struct HullBreachEvent {
    Entity room;
    float forceStrength;
    float duration;
};
Hull Breach System
class HullBreachSystem {
public:
    void Trigger(const HullBreachEvent& event) {
        breachedRoom = event.room;
        force = event.forceStrength;
        timer = event.duration;

        EventBus::Emit(AudioEvent{"HULL_BREACH"});
        EventBus::Emit(EnvironmentEvent{"ZERO_G_ON"});
        EventBus::Emit(CameraEvent{"SHAKE_HEAVY"});
    }

    void Tick(float dt) {
        if (timer <= 0.f) return;

        timer -= dt;

        ApplySuctionForces();
        PullLooseObjects();

        if (timer <= 0.f)
            Resolve();
    }

private:
    Entity breachedRoom;
    float force;
    float timer;

    void ApplySuctionForces() {
        for (Entity e : ecs.Query<PhysicsComponent>(breachedRoom)) {
            ecs.Get<PhysicsComponent>(e).velocity +=
                BreachNormal * force;
        }
    }

    void Resolve() {
        EventBus::Emit(EnvironmentEvent{"ZERO_G_OFF"});
        EventBus::Emit(AudioEvent{"EMERGENCY_ALARM_STOP"});
    }
};
Reusable anywhere:

Weapons fire

Reactor meltdown

Scripted mission beats

3️⃣ ENEMY BEHAVIOR TREES (LEAN & READABLE)
No black-box AI. These are data-driven trees.

Enemy State Component
enum class EnemyCombatState {
    IDLE,
    AWARE,
    ATTACKING,
    TAKING_COVER,
    RETREATING,
    DEAD
};

struct EnemyAIComponent {
    EnemyCombatState state = EnemyCombatState::IDLE;
    float bravery;
    float health;
};
Behavior Tree Logic (Core)
class EnemyAISystem {
public:
    void Tick(Entity enemy, float dt) {
        auto& ai = ecs.Get<EnemyAIComponent>(enemy);

        if (ai.health <= 0.f) {
            ai.state = EnemyCombatState::DEAD;
            return;
        }

        switch (ai.state) {
            case EnemyCombatState::IDLE:
                if (CanSeePlayer(enemy))
                    ai.state = EnemyCombatState::AWARE;
                break;

            case EnemyCombatState::AWARE:
                ai.state = EnemyCombatState::ATTACKING;
                break;

            case EnemyCombatState::ATTACKING:
                if (UnderHeavyFire(enemy))
                    ai.state = EnemyCombatState::TAKING_COVER;
                else
                    FireAtPlayer(enemy);
                break;

            case EnemyCombatState::TAKING_COVER:
                MoveToCover(enemy);
                if (ai.health < 30.f && ai.bravery < 0.5f)
                    ai.state = EnemyCombatState::RETREATING;
                else
                    ai.state = EnemyCombatState::ATTACKING;
                break;

            case EnemyCombatState::RETREATING:
                FallBackTowardObjective(enemy);
                break;
        }
    }
};
✔ No teleporting
✔ Player can read intent
✔ Cheap CPU

4️⃣ AUDIO EVENT DISPATCHER (CRITICAL GLUE)
This is the nervous system.

Audio Event Definition
struct AudioEvent {
    std::string eventName;
    Entity source = INVALID_ENTITY;
};
Audio Dispatcher
class AudioEventDispatcher {
public:
    void OnEvent(const AudioEvent& e) {
        auto def = audioTable[e.eventName];

        PlaySound(def.clip,
                  def.volume,
                  def.reverb,
                  e.source);

        if (def.duckMusic)
            DuckMusic(def.duckAmount);
    }

private:
    struct AudioDef {
        std::string clip;
        float volume;
        std::string reverb;
        bool duckMusic;
        float duckAmount;
    };

    std::unordered_map<std::string, AudioDef> audioTable;
};
Example Audio Table Entry
audioTable["HULL_BREACH"] = {
    "sfx/hull_breach.wav",
    1.0f,
    "HALL",
    true,
    0.4f
};
Audio Priority Rules (LOCKED)
Breathing overrides ambience

Hull breach overrides everything

Silence after breach = intentional

Music resumes slowly (2–3s fade)
